***-ie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a> (6074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-ia</i>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_3">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="derivedterms CategoryTreeTag" data-ct-mode="10" data-ct-options="{quot;modequot;:10,quot;hideprefixquot;:20,quot;showcountquot;:false,quot;namespacesquot;:[0],quot;notranslationsquot;:false}"><div class="CategoryTreeSection"><div class="CategoryTreeItem"><span class="CategoryTreeBullet"><span class="CategoryTreeToggle" data-ct-title="Dutch_words_suffixed_with_-ie_(variant_of_-ij)" data-ct-state="collapsed">►</span> </span> Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> suffixed with <a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a> (variant of -ij)</div><div class="CategoryTreeChildren" style="display:none"></div></div></div>
<p><br />
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-iō</i>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_4">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="derivedterms CategoryTreeTag" data-ct-mode="10" data-ct-options="{quot;modequot;:10,quot;hideprefixquot;:20,quot;showcountquot;:false,quot;namespacesquot;:[0],quot;notranslationsquot;:false}"><div class="CategoryTreeSection"><div class="CategoryTreeItem"><span class="CategoryTreeBullet"><span class="CategoryTreeToggle" data-ct-title="Dutch_words_suffixed_with_-ie_(process_or_condition)" data-ct-state="collapsed">►</span> </span> Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> suffixed with <a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a> (process or condition)</div><div class="CategoryTreeChildren" style="display:none"></div></div></div>
<p><br />
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>An alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></i> in popular speech.
</p>

<dl><dd>«Players of word games like <a href = vnd.unilang:scrabble.html>Scrabble</a> like <b>aa</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> if they do not know what it means.»

***aaa.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> aaa (11369)</h1><br></body> 
***aaaaah.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aaaaah.html>aaaaah</a> (85426)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>Indication of amazement or surprise or enthusiasm.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>Aah</a>!</b> That's amazing!</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1985</b>,  Joan Morrison,  chapter 5, in  <cite>Share House Blues</cite>, Boolarong Publications, page 62:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">'<b><a href = vnd.unilang:aaah.html>Aaah</a></b>!' they sigh, as the silvery Space Shuttle <a href = vnd.unilang:races.html>races</a> heavenwards on top of a towering pillar of flame.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Indication of joyful pleasure.
<ul><li><b>1834</b> — <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edgar_Allan_Poe" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edgar Allan Poe"><a href = vnd.unilang:edgar.html>Edgar</a> Allan Poe</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Assignation" class="extiw" title="s:The Assignation">The Assignation</a></i>
<dl><dd>Yet I remember—<b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a>!</b> how should I forget?</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Indication of sympathy.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>Aah</a></b>, I feel so bad for you...</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Indication of mouth being opened wide.
<dl><dd><i>Dentists would always instruct, say <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a>!</b></i></dd></dl></li>
<li>To express understanding.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>Aah</a></b>. Now I understand.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>The sound of one <a href = vnd.unilang:screaming.html>screaming</a> (with as many a's or h's as needed for emphasis).
<dl><dd><i><b>AAAHHH</b>! A bug! A bug! Get it off <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>! Get it off <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>!</i></dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>Aah</a></b>! A <a href = vnd.unilang:rat.html>rat</a>!</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">aahs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Expression of amazement, surprise, enthusiasm, or fear.</li>
<li>Expression of joy and/or pleasure.</li>
<li>The exclamation <a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">aahs</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">aahing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">aahed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To say or exclaim <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></b>.
<ol><li>To express amazement or surprise or enthusiasm, especially by the interjection <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></b>.
<dl><dd><i>Everyone who <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> by oohed and <b>aahed</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> her new appearance.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>To express joy or pleasure, especially by the interjection <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></b>.</li></ol></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The object of <a href = vnd.unilang:feelings.html>feelings</a> usually <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> indicated by the prepositions <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> or at.</li>
<li>Very often the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used together with some other verb derived from an interjection. The most common combination <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i>to <a href = vnd.unilang:ooh.html>ooh</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></i>.</li></ul>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aagje.html>aagje</a> (41174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Name derived from <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:agatha.html>Agatha</a></span>, from a farce <a href = vnd.unilang:dating.html>dating</a> back to 1653 " '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwsgierig.html>Nieuwsgierig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aagje.html>Aagje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Enkhuizen.", Curious <a href = vnd.unilang:agatha.html>Agatha</a> from Enkhuizen'
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aagje.html>aagje</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>a very curious person, "<a href = vnd.unilang:paulina.html>Paulina</a> Pry".</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***aah.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a> (13051)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>Indication of amazement or surprise or enthusiasm.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>Aah</a>!</b> That's amazing!</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1985</b>,  Joan Morrison,  chapter 5, in  <cite>Share House Blues</cite>, Boolarong Publications, page 62:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">'<b><a href = vnd.unilang:aaah.html>Aaah</a></b>!' they sigh, as the silvery Space Shuttle <a href = vnd.unilang:races.html>races</a> heavenwards on top of a towering pillar of flame.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Indication of joyful pleasure.
<ul><li><b>1834</b> — <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edgar_Allan_Poe" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edgar Allan Poe"><a href = vnd.unilang:edgar.html>Edgar</a> Allan Poe</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Assignation" class="extiw" title="s:The Assignation">The Assignation</a></i>
<dl><dd>Yet I remember—<b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a>!</b> how should I forget?</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Indication of sympathy.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>Aah</a></b>, I feel so bad for you...</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Indication of mouth being opened wide.
<dl><dd><i>Dentists would always instruct, say <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a>!</b></i></dd></dl></li>
<li>To express understanding.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>Aah</a></b>. Now I understand.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>The sound of one <a href = vnd.unilang:screaming.html>screaming</a> (with as many a's or h's as needed for emphasis).
<dl><dd><i><b>AAAHHH</b>! A bug! A bug! Get it off <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>! Get it off <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>!</i></dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>Aah</a></b>! A <a href = vnd.unilang:rat.html>rat</a>!</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">aahs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Expression of amazement, surprise, enthusiasm, or fear.</li>
<li>Expression of joy and/or pleasure.</li>
<li>The exclamation <a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">aahs</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">aahing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">aahed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To say or exclaim <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></b>.
<ol><li>To express amazement or surprise or enthusiasm, especially by the interjection <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></b>.
<dl><dd><i>Everyone who <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> by oohed and <b>aahed</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> her new appearance.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>To express joy or pleasure, especially by the interjection <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></b>.</li></ol></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The object of <a href = vnd.unilang:feelings.html>feelings</a> usually <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> indicated by the prepositions <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> or at.</li>
<li>Very often the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used together with some other verb derived from an interjection. The most common combination <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i>to <a href = vnd.unilang:ooh.html>ooh</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:aah.html>aah</a></i>.</li></ul>
</body>

***aak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aak.html>aak</a> (85424)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aecke</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">naecke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nako</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nakwô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boat, ship</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***aal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aal.html>aal</a> (27285)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">âel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*āl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ēlaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aal.html>aal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alen.html>alen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aal.html>aaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">eel</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">fish</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, (<i>Anguilla anguilla</i>)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">elver</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">young eel</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">padre</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:aal.html>Aal</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the original word for eel used in the present-day Netherlands, while the word <i><a href = vnd.unilang:paling.html>paling</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> from Belgium. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:paling.html>Paling</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also in use in the Netherlands, but certain fishing villages in the Netherlands such as Volendam will always use <i><a href = vnd.unilang:aal.html>aal</a></i> when referring to eel. In some regions <i><a href = vnd.unilang:aal.html>aal</a></i> always denotes a juvenile whereas <i><a href = vnd.unilang:paling.html>paling</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> exclusively used for adult specimen.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paling.html>paling</a></span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">aalfuik</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">aalkorf</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aalscholver.html>aalscholver</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">beefaal</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">glasaal</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">āle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*alo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*alu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂elut-</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ale.html>ale</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aal.html>aal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alen.html>alen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aal.html>aaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ale.html>ale</a></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:adel.html>adel</a></i>, 'mud'.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aal.html>aal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">glad</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slippery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aal.html>aal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">scholver</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cormorant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aalscholver.html>aalscholver</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aalscholvers.html>aalscholvers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aalscholver.html>aalscholvertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cormorant (<i>a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of seabird</i>)
<ul><li><b>1825</b>, Jacobus Scheltema, "<a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>Iets</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> boetseerkunst, in <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>heer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:petrus.html>Petrus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koning.html>Koning</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:utrecht.html>Utrecht</a>", in <i>Mengelwerk</i> (edition of <i>Vaderlandsche letteroefeningen</i>), 665.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> geopende <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aalscholver.html>aalscholver</a></b> of aalslokker (<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> palingdief), <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geslacht.html>geslacht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> pellikanen behoorende, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voornaamste.html>voornaamste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stukken.html>stukken</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:opmerkelijk.html>opmerkelijk</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aambei.html>aambei</a> (61975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenbey</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on; to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bei.html>bei</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">berry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Assimilation of <i>-n-</i> to <i>-m-</i> before <i>-b</i>, like in <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aambeeld.html>aambeeld</a></i> from <i>aanbeeld</i>.
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">aanbidd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanbidden.html>aanbidden</a></i></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.

***aanblik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanblik.html>aanblik</a> (14076)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenblic</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blik.html>blik</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanblik.html>aanblik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanblik.html>aanblikken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanblik.html>aanblikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>appearance, aspect</li></ol>

***aandachtig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aandachtig.html>aandachtig</a> (13511)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aandacht.html>aandacht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">attention, care</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">y, -ive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; perfectly parallel with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">andächtig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aandachtig.html>aandachtig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aandachtig.html>aandachtiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">aandachtigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(of a person) attentive, paying care/attention</li>
<li>(of an object) careful, enjoying care/attention <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(clarification of this definition <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> needed)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">āendienen</i>. </p>

***aangaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aangaan.html>aangaan</a> (7137)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">āengâan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">anagān</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">angehen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aangaan.html>aangaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be a concern to, to concern
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My comings and goings <b>are</b> not <b>your concern</b> at all.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to enter (into something), to begin (something)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> contract <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedrijf.html>bedrijf</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <b>entered into</b> a contract with the company.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start, to turn on <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a machine or device, or lights</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> computer <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aangaan.html>aangaan</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:bleek.html>Bleek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stekker.html>stekker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stopcontact.html>stopcontact</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The computer just wouldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>start</b>. Turns out the plug wasn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> plugged into the power outlet.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in early Dutch  impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to befall, to happen to</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go to (someone), to approach (someone)</li></ol>
